<ol start="3">
<li>To deploy your project, you'll need to push your code to a Git repository (like GitHub) and then connect it to Netlify. Here's how you can initialize a Git repository and push your code:</li>
</ol>

<ol start="4">
<li>
<p>After pushing your code to GitHub, follow these steps:</p>
<ul>
<li>Go to <a href="https://www.netlify.com/">Netlify</a> and sign up or log in</li>
<li>Click "New site from Git"</li>
<li>Choose GitHub and select your repository</li>
<li>In the deploy settings, leave the defaults (Build command: <code>npm run build</code>, Publish directory: <code>dist</code>)</li>
<li>Click "Deploy site"</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Netlify will now build and deploy your site. Once it's done, you'll get a URL like <code>https://your-site-name.netlify.app</code>. This is the link you can share with others to show your creativity!</p>
</li>
</ol>
